    const isLocalized = (path) => {
        return path.match(/^\/?\w{2}-\w{2}/) !== null;
    };

    const getMarketFromUrl = (url) =>
        new URL(url)?.pathname
            ?.split('/')
            ?.at(1)
            ?.match(/^\w+-([\w-]+)$/)
            ?.at(1) ?? null;

    const removeUrlLocalization = (path) => {
        let normalizedPath = path;

        if (normalizedPath.startsWith('/')) {
            normalizedPath = normalizedPath.slice(1);
        }

        if (isLocalized(normalizedPath)) {
            return '/' + normalizedPath.split('/').slice(1).join('/');
        }

        return '/' + normalizedPath;
    };

    const removeStartingSlash = (url) => {
        return url.startsWith('/') ? url.slice(1) : url;
    };

            appeaserCountryConfig[countryCode.toLocaleLowerCase()] || appeaserCountryConfig.ww;
        const marketCode =

            marketConfig[currentMarketCode].countries.includes(countryCode.toLocaleLowerCase()),

        const lang =
            applicationLanguage && appeaserConfig?.locales[applicationLanguage.toLocaleLowerCase()]
            ? appeaserConfig.locales[applicationLanguage.toLocaleLowerCase()]
            : appeaserConfig?.defaultLocale;

            lang ?? fallbackLang,
            appeaserConfig?.country?.toLocaleUpperCase() || countryCode?.toLocaleUpperCase(),
        ].join('_');

                documentReferrerSearchParam,
                originSearchParamsAsString,

        }
    }

        ?.split('; ')
        .reduce((prev, current) => {
            const [name, ...value] = current.split('=');

            return prev;

src="https://www.cos.com/akam/13/pixel_3d4537bc?a=dD1kYTA2ZTFkNDQzYWJkOThmMTI5ZDhlNWU1NjE0M2Q5MzI5Y2U0YmU2JmpzPW9mZg==" style="visibility: hidden; position: absolute; left: -999px; top: -999px;"     function OptanonWrapper() {
        if (typeof window === 'undefined') {
            return;
        }

        // Add both cookie banner links
        const cookiePolicyLinkElement = document.querySelector('footer a[href*="/cookie"]');
        const cookiePolicyLink = cookiePolicyLinkElement?.href || '';
        const oneTrustBannerPolicyLinkElement = document.getElementById('onetrust-banner-cookie-policy-link');
        if (oneTrustBannerPolicyLinkElement) {
            oneTrustBannerPolicyLinkElement.href = cookiePolicyLink;
            oneTrustBannerPolicyLinkElement.target = "_self";
        }
        const oneTrustPcPolicyLinkElement = document.getElementById('onetrust-pc-cookie-policy-link');
        if (oneTrustPcPolicyLinkElement) {
            oneTrustPcPolicyLinkElement.href = cookiePolicyLink;
            oneTrustPcPolicyLinkElement.target = "_self";
        }

        // Hide initial banner when cookie settings is opened and enable escape button functionality
        const oneTrustBanner = document.getElementById('onetrust-banner-sdk');
        if (oneTrustBanner) {
            // Read more/less button functionality
            const readMoreButton = document.getElementById("read-more-button");
            const readLessButton = document.getElementById("read-less-button");
            const readMoreCheckbox = document.getElementById("read-more-toggle");

            if (readMoreButton && readMoreCheckbox) {
                readMoreButton.addEventListener("click", () => {
                    readMoreCheckbox.checked = true;
                    readMoreButton.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");
                    const policyText = document.getElementById("onetrust-policy-text");
                    if (policyText) {
                        policyText.querySelectorAll("a").forEach(link => {
                            link.setAttribute("tabindex", "0");
                        });
                    }
                });
            }

            if (readLessButton && readMoreCheckbox) {
                readLessButton.addEventListener("click", () => {
                    readMoreCheckbox.checked = false;
                    readMoreButton.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                    const policyText = document.getElementById("onetrust-policy-text");
                    if (policyText) {
                        policyText.querySelectorAll("a").forEach(link => {
                            link.setAttribute("tabindex", "-1");
                        });
                    }
                });
            }

            const oneTrustOpenButton = document.getElementById('onetrust-pc-btn-handler');
            if (oneTrustOpenButton) {
                oneTrustOpenButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    oneTrustBanner.style.display = "none";
                });
            }
            const oneTrustCloseButton = document.getElementById('close-pc-btn-handler');
            if (oneTrustCloseButton) {
                oneTrustCloseButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    oneTrustBanner.style.display = "block";
                });
            }
            
            document.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
                if (oneTrustBanner.style.display === "none" && (event.key === "Escape" || event.key === "Esc")) {
                    oneTrustBanner.style.display = "block";
                }
            });
        }

        // Fix incorrect height set to cookie settings '.ot-pc-content' element
        const oneTrustPc = document.getElementById('onetrust-pc-sdk');
        if (oneTrustPc) {
            const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
                mutations.forEach((mutation) => {
                    if (mutation.attributeName === "class" && 
                        mutation.target.classList.contains("ot-animated", "ot-slide-in-left")) {
                        const oneTrustFooter = oneTrustPc.querySelector(".ot-pc-footer");
                        if (oneTrustFooter) {
                            const oneTrustPcHeight = oneTrustPc.offsetHeight;
                            const oneTrustFooterHeight = oneTrustFooter.offsetHeight;
                            const content = oneTrustPc.querySelector("#ot-pc-content");
                            if (content) {
                                content.style.height = `${oneTrustPcHeight - oneTrustFooterHeight}px`;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });
            });
            observer.observe(oneTrustPc, { attributes: true });
        }
    }
